<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Dido and Aeneas
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Dido and Ãneas
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Purcell,_Henry" title="Category:Purcell, Henry">Purcell, Henry</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Z.626
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IHP 11
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts
<dl><dd>Overture
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act I
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Solo and Chorus: Shake the Cloud
</dd><dd>2. Song: Ah! Belinda
</dd><dd>3. Recitative: Grief Increases
</dd><dd>4. Chorus: When Monarchs Unite
</dd><dd>5. Recitative: Whence Could so Much Virtue Spring
</dd><dd>6. Duet and Chorus: Fear No Danger
</dd><dd>7. Recitative: See Your Royal Guest
</dd><dd>8. Chorus: Cupid Only
</dd><dd>9. Recitative: If Not for Mine
</dd><dd>10. Air: Persue Thy Conquest
</dd><dd>11. Chorus: To the Hills and the Vales
</dd><dd>12: The Triumphing Dance
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act II
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>13. Prelude for the Witches
</dd><dd>14. Chorus: Harm's Our Delight
</dd><dd>15. Recitative: The Queen of Carthage
</dd><dd>16. Chorus: Ho! Ho! Ho!
</dd><dd>17. Recitative: Ruin'd Ere the Set of Sun
</dd><dd>18. Chorus: Ho! Ho! Ho!
</dd><dd>19. Duet: But, Ere we This Perform
</dd><dd>20. Chorus: In Our Deep Vaulted Cell
</dd><dd>21. Echo Dance of Furies
</dd><dd>22. Ritornelle
</dd><dd>23. Song and Chorus: Thanks to These Lonesome Vales
</dd><dd>24. Song: Oft She Visits
</dd><dd>25. Recitative: Behold, Upon My Bended Spear
</dd><dd>26. Song and Chorus: Haste to Town
</dd><dd>27. Recitative: Stay, Prince
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Act III
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>28. Prelude, Song and Chorus: Come Away, Fellow Sailors
</dd><dd>29. The Sailors' Dance
</dd><dd>30a. Recitative: See the Flags
</dd><dd>30b. Song: Our Next Motion Must Be to Storm
</dd><dd>31. Chorus: Destruction's Our Delight
</dd><dd>32. The Witches' Dance
</dd><dd>33. Recitative: Your Counsel
</dd><dd>34. Recitative: But Death, Alas!
</dd><dd>35. Chorus: Great Minds
</dd><dd>36. Recitative: Thy Hand, Belinda
</dd><dd>37. Song: When I am Laid in Earth
</dd><dd>38. With Drooping Wings
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
